
# 🚀 Harika GPT Image 2 İstemleri

[![Awesome](https://awesome.re/badge.svg)](https://github.com/sindresorhus/awesome)
[![License: CC BY 4.0](https://img.shields.io/badge/License-CC%20BY%204.0-lightgrey.svg)](https://creativecommons.org/licenses/by/4.0/)
[![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AtlasCloudAI/awesome-gpt-image-2-prompts?style=social)](https://github.com/AtlasCloudAI/awesome-gpt-image-2-prompts)
[![PRs Welcome](https://img.shields.io/badge/PRs-welcome-brightgreen.svg)](docs/CONTRIBUTING.md)
[![Prompts](https://img.shields.io/badge/prompts-1100%2B-blue.svg)](https://www.atlascloud.ai/prompts-hub/gpt-image-2-prompt?utm_source=github&utm_campaign=awesome-gpt-image-2-prompts)

> 🎨 OpenAI'nin GPT Image 2'si için yaratıcı istemler koleksiyonu — with **real previews generated via Atlas Cloud**.

> ⚠️ **Telif Hakkı Bildirimi**: Tüm istemler eğitim amaçlı olarak topluluktan toplanmıştır. Herhangi bir içeriğin haklarınızı ihlal ettiğini düşünüyorsanız, lütfen [bir sorun açın](https://github.com/AtlasCloudAI/awesome-gpt-image-2-prompts/issues/new?template=bug-report.yml) ve derhal kaldıralım.

### 🧩 Supported Models

- 🎬 **Video** — Seedance 2.0 · Kling 3 · Sora 2 · Veo 3.1 · HappyHorse 1 · Grok Imagine 1.5 · Wan 2.7
- 🎨 **Image** — Nano Banana 2/Pro · GPT Image 2 · Flux 2 · Seedream 5
- 💬 **LLM** — Claude · GPT · DeepSeek · MiniMax · Kimi · GLM · Qwen
- 🔊 **Audio** — Grok TTS
- 📚 **Explore more** — [300+ models »](https://www.atlascloud.ai/models?utm_source=github&utm_campaign=awesome-gpt-image-2-prompts)

**▶ Run any prompt via Atlas Cloud**

- 🧠 **Skill (recommended)** — install [atlas-cloud-skills](https://github.com/AtlasCloudAI/atlas-cloud-skills) in Claude Code / Codex / Gemini CLI, then ask: *"Generate this with GPT Image 2 on Atlas Cloud: &lt;paste a prompt&gt;"*.
- 💻 **CLI** — prefer the terminal? Use [atlascloud-cli](https://github.com/AtlasCloudAI/cli).
- 🔑 **[Get a free API key →](https://www.atlascloud.ai/console/api-keys?utm_source=github&utm_campaign=awesome-gpt-image-2-prompts)** · 300+ models, one key.

## 🤔 GPT Image 2 nedir?

**GPT Image 2** (codename **"duct-tape"**) is OpenAI's next-generation image model. Community testing highlights a leap in these areas:

- 🎯 **Pixel-Perfect Text Rendering** — Native-quality text in Chinese, English, and Japanese, no typos or warped glyphs
- 🎨 **Cross-Image Consistency** — The same character, style, or IP stays identical across a series, down to the pixel
- ⚡ **Commercial-Grade Illustration** — Illustration output is ready to ship without manual polish
- 🌈 **True Art Style Induction** — Creatively evokes the feeling of a style rather than merely approximating references
- 🔧 **Storyboard & Product Series** — Ideal for storyboards, IP characters, and multi-panel product visuals
- 📐 **Multi-Language Design** — Social cards, banners, and posters with accurate multilingual typography in one shot

📚 **Learn More:** See community testing in our [report summary](docs/FAQ.md)

### 🚀 Raycast Entegrasyonu

Bazı istemler [Raycast Snippets](https://raycast.com/help/snippets) sözdizimini kullanarak **dinamik argümanlar** destekler. 🚀 Raycast Friendly rozetini arayın!

**Örnek:**
```
A quote card with "{argument name="quote" default="Stay hungry, stay foolish"}"
by {argument name="author" default="Steve Jobs"}
```

Raycast'te kullanıldığında, hızlı yinelemeler için argümanları dinamik olarak değiştirebilirsiniz!

> ⭐ Ekibimiz tarafından olağanüstü kalite ve yaratıcılık için özenle seçildi

### No. 1: Sıcak 4 Panel Evli Çift Mangası

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/⭐-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Bu istem, evli bir çifti kutlayan yumuşak, romantik dört panelli bir Japon çizgi romanı oluşturur; sosyal paylaşımlar, anma illüstrasyonları veya ilişki temalı manga sanatı için idealdir.

#### 📝 İstem

```
{"type":"4-panel romantic manga illustration","style":"clean hand-drawn anime line art with a warm beige and light brown monochrome palette, soft cream background, simple shading, cozy and gentle atmosphere, social media post aesthetic","format":"square 2x2 comic layout with thin brown panel borders","headline":{"text":"{argument name=\"headline text\" default=\"夫婦の日\"}","position":"top center","decorations":{"count":2,"items":["small heart on the left","small heart on the right"]}},"panels":[{"panel":1,"count":2,"scene":"standing portrait of a young couple","composition":"the man stands behind the woman with one hand on her shoulder, both looking calm and affectionate","characters":[{"role":"man","appearance":"messy light brown hair, glasses, cream hoodie, tall and slim"},{"role":"woman","appearance":"light brown hair in a loose low bun with strands framing the face, white long-sleeve shirt, warm brown sweater vest, shoulder bag strap visible"}],"text":["今日は","夫婦の日！"],"decorations":{"count":3,"items":["small heart","small heart","small heart"]}},{"panel":2,"count":2,"scene":"the couple sitting together indoors holding mugs and smiling at each other","characters":[{"role":"man","appearance":"same glasses and hoodie, holding a muted green mug"},{"role":"woman","appearance":"same hairstyle and outfit, holding a light mug"}],"speech_bubble":{"speaker":"man","text":"いつもありがとう。 一緒にいられることが、 いちばんの幸せだよ。"},"decorations":{"count":4,"items":["small sparkle","small sparkle","small dot cluster","small dot cluster"]}},{"panel":3,"count":2,"scene":"the couple cooking together in a kitchen, both stirring a pan on the stove","background":"simple shelves and potted plant in soft sketchy detail","characters":[{"role":"man","appearance":"same glasses and hoodie"},{"role":"woman","appearance":"same bun hairstyle and layered outfit"}],"speech_bubble":{"speaker":"man","text":"これからも、 笑い合って、支え合って、 一緒にいろんな景色を 見ていこうね。"}},{"panel":4,"count":2,"scene":"close affectionate embrace, the man kisses the woman on the forehead while holding her shoulder","characters":[{"role":"man","appearance":"same glasses and hoodie"},{"role":"woman","appearance":"same hair and outfit, leaning into him"}],"speech_bubble":{"speaker":"man","text":"大好きだよ。 これからも、 よろしくね！"},"decorations":{"count":3,"items":["small heart","small heart","small heart"]}}],"footer":{"text":"{argument name=\"footer text\" default=\"いつもそばにいてくれて、ありがとう。\"}","position":"bottom center","decorations":{"count":1,"items":["small heart"]}},"character_design":{"count":2,"items":[{"role":"husband","hair color":"{argument name=\"hair color\" default=\"light brown\"}","expression":"kind, gentle, affectionate"},{"role":"wife","hair color":"{argument name=\"hair color\" default=\"light brown\"}","expression":"soft smile, loving, slightly shy"}]},"rendering_notes":"keep all text handwritten in Japanese, use lots of white space, preserve a sweet commemorative mood for a couple's appreciation post, make the linework slightly loose and sketchlike rather than polished ink"}

### No. 2: Sevimli Siyah Yavru Kedi Japon Çıkartma Sayfası

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/⭐-Featured-gold)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Japonca ifadeler içeren, ifade dolu bir siyah yavru kedinin 15 panelli çıkartma tarzı sayfası; sohbet çıkartmaları, LINE pul konseptleri veya sosyal medya görselleri için ideal.

#### 📝 İstem

```
{"type":"cute sticker sheet illustration","subject":{"species":"black kitten","style":"adorable chibi, soft painterly anime-cartoon look, big round amber-brown eyes, tiny muzzle, expressive ears, fluffy dark charcoal-black fur with warm brown highlights, thick clean outline"},"layout":{"background":"plain white","grid":{"rows":3,"columns":5,"count":15},"sections":[{"title":"01. ありがとう！","position":"row 1 col 1","count":1,"labels":["happy grateful pose with both paws clasped at chest, open smiling mouth, pink cherry blossom petals around the cat"]},{"title":"02. おつかれさま！","position":"row 1 col 2","count":1,"labels":["content relaxed cat holding a green mug with a paw-print emblem, eyes closed, small puff of steam, celebratory yellow accent lines"]},{"title":"03. 了解です！","position":"row 1 col 3","count":1,"labels":["upright kitten raising one paw in acknowledgment, bright attentive expression, yellow accent lines above"]},{"title":"04. ＯＫ！","position":"row 1 col 4","count":1,"labels":["winking kitten making an OK hand gesture with one paw, slight smile, yellow accent lines"]},{"title":"05. はーい！","position":"row 1 col 5","count":1,"labels":["excited kitten waving one paw high, open smiling mouth, yellow accent lines"]},{"title":"06. いいね！","position":"row 2 col 1","count":1,"labels":["winking kitten giving a thumbs-up, small pink heart beside it, yellow accent lines"]},{"title":"07. がんばる！","position":"row 2 col 2","count":1,"labels":["determined kitten with clenched paws and fierce eyes, surrounded by stylized orange flames"]},{"title":"08. なんとかなる！","position":"row 2 col 3","count":1,"labels":["confident serene kitten with eyes closed and chest slightly puffed out, pink blossoms floating around"]},{"title":"09. ごめんね…","position":"row 2 col 4","count":1,"labels":["apologetic sad kitten with paws held together at chest, droopy eyes, one blue sweat drop"]},{"title":"10. 待ってるね！","position":"row 2 col 5","count":1,"labels":["kitten peeking over a wooden ledge with both paws visible, expectant expression, small motion lines on both sides"]},{"title":"11. ### No. 4: Kahverengi Tonlarda Samat Butik Portresi

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)

#### 📝 İstem

```
A candid, photorealistic vertical smartphone photo of a young East Asian woman standing in a warm-toned boutique or home fragrance shop, shot from a slightly high angle looking down at her upper body and torso. She has {argument name="hair color" default="dark brown to black"} hair tied back in a low ponytail with a few loose strands near the face, and she is holding a small creamy-white cup or candle jar close to her mouth with one hand. She wears a very fitted ribbed zip-front long-sleeve top in {argument name="outfit color" default="chocolate brown"}, partially unzipped, paired with matching high-waisted pants in the same brown tone for a monochrome look. Her pose is casual and slightly leaning, with the other arm relaxed behind her back, giving the image an off-guard lifestyle snapshot feeling. The store shelves around her are wooden and filled with many glass candle jars and small product containers, softly blurred in the background and along the left side of the frame. Use warm indoor ambient lighting, shallow depth of field, realistic skin texture, subtle highlights on the hair, natural hand pose, and a cozy artisanal retail atmosphere. Compose it as a tight mid-to-full body crop in portrait orientation, with the subject centered and the background angled diagonally to enhance the candid perspective. Photographic style: realistic, high-detail, soft bokeh, boutique shopping snapshot, 35mm lens look, natural color grading.
```

### No. 5: Cyberpunk Çatı Baskını

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/⭐-Featured-gold)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Bu prompt, yağmurlu, neon ışıklı bir çatıda bir kapıyı zorlayan beş kişilik bir taktiksel ekibin yer aldığı, dramatik geniş bir cyberpunk aksiyon sahnesi oluşturur; distopik bilimkurgu konsept sanatı veya sinematik oyun görselleri için ideal.

#### 📝 İstem

```
A cinematic cyberpunk night raid on a rain-soaked rooftop balcony in a dense futuristic megacity, viewed in a wide-angle shot from slightly behind and to the side of the squad. Five heavily armed tactical soldiers in black futuristic body armor and full helmets stack at a metal door on the far left: 1 soldier is actively breaching the door with one boot raised and bright orange sparks exploding outward, 1 soldier stands just behind aiming into the doorway, 1 soldier crouches low in the center with rifle ready, 1 soldier stands mid-right aiming across the balcony toward the city, and 1 soldier kneels in the right foreground behind the railing. The environment is packed with towering skyscrapers, elevated skybridges, distant traffic lanes, wet reflective metal surfaces, drifting steam, rain haze, and a deep blue-black stormy sky. Neon signage and giant billboards dominate the scene in magenta, cyan, violet, and electric blue, including visible signs reading "POCARI SWEAT" twice, "softsys", "DATA INC", "ROSE", "BARIKI", "2F", "KIROSHI", and multiple vertical Japanese and Chinese-style neon signs. Include 2 hovering flying vehicles in the mid-distance sky and countless illuminated windows receding into the background. The overall mood should feel gritty, moody, high-contrast, and slightly glitchy, with nostalgic old-school AI-art instability: some billboard portraits are malformed or partially censored by soft purple rectangular blocks, a few signs feel inconsistent, and fine architectural details subtly smear or repeat. Emphasize wet reflections, volumetric fog, sparks, rim lighting on the soldiers, dense urban depth, and a dramatic action-movie composition in the style of a dystopian sci-fi concept art keyframe.
```

### No. 5: Vahşi Fantezi Savaşçısı ve Kurt

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Bu prompt, süslü zırh, mızrak ve bir kurt yoldaşıyla birlikte sinematik tam vücut bir fantezi kadın kahraman portresi oluşturur; epik karakter sanatı ve karanlık fantezi ana görselleri için idealdir.

#### 📝 İstem

```
A cinematic fantasy portrait of a fierce female warrior walking forward across a rugged, sunlit wilderness at golden hour, accompanied by 1 large wolf at her right side. She is the central full-body subject, tall and powerful, with long wind-whipped {argument name="hair color" default="deep copper red"} hair streaming dramatically to the left, and 1 ornate metallic feather-like headpiece at the side of her head. Her face is partially obscured or de-emphasized, keeping the focus on silhouette, hair, armor, and mood. She wears elaborate biomechanical-elven armor in pale ivory, silver, and muted champagne tones, highly detailed with filigree, engraved lines, layered plates, gemstone settings, delicate chainwork, and fitted feminine contours; the armor includes 1 sculpted breastplate, 2 armored pauldrons, 2 engraved bracers, 1 jeweled belt centerpiece, 2 thigh guards, and 2 intricately plated greaves. Flowing from the armor are torn translucent fabric panels and a long ember-red cape or veil that trails behind her in ribbons, catching the light like sparks. In her right hand she carries 1 tall ceremonial spear-staff with an ornate bladed head, dangling chains, and red gem accents. The wolf is lean, alert, and battle-adorned, wearing matching decorative harness armor with etched metallic details and red markings, moving in step beside her. The environment is an open rocky plain with distant hills or mountains, dry grasses, floating dust, and glowing particles throughout the scene. Use dramatic backlighting, warm amber sunlight, high contrast, shallow atmospheric haze, hyper-detailed textures, fantasy realism, epic dark-golden palette, dynamic motion in hair and cloth, and a majestic untamed mood in the style of a premium gpt-image-2 fantasy character key visual. No text, no logo, no watermark.
```

```

On the left is a USA countryball with angry narrowed eyes, painted with the American flag, wearing a dark navy baseball cap labeled "USA" in large white letters. On the right is an Iran countryball with angry narrowed eyes, painted with the Iranian flag and emblem, wearing a green-and-white headband tied on the side; the headband contains Korean text that reads "저항은 우리의 권리". On the right cliff, include exactly 1 warning sign with Persian text at the top and a red warning triangle below, indicating that only one person can pass. In the left bottom corner, place exactly 1 black oil barrel labeled "OIL" with dark spilled oil pooling around it. In the right bottom corner, place exactly 1 black naval mine with Persian writing on it, attached to a chain. In the background beyond the narrow passage, show open sea with exactly 3 distant ships, including at least 1 larger tanker and faint dark smoke rising into the sky. Use a tense but humorous geopolitical meme tone, centered composition, eye-level view, soft daylight, slightly muted realistic colors, crisp outlines, and high readability for all text.

```
A dramatic Japanese fantasy movie poster in a painterly, ultra-detailed cinematic illustration style. The poster is vertically composed like a theatrical key visual, with a warm gold title at the bottom and multiple emotional vignettes layered into one unified scene. The central character is a small fluffy pig-like creature with soft pale cream fur, oversized pink inner ears, a tiny snout, a curled tail, and large feathered angel wings glowing with golden light. It stands upright on a rooftop or elevated wooden platform overlooking a vast Tokyo cityscape at sunset, holding a whiskey glass in one hoof with the other hoof on its hip, posed like a weary but resilient middle-aged salaryman. The whole image should feel bittersweet, magical, lonely, and hopeful, like a prestige animated film poster about adulthood, solitude, and emotional survival. Use lush lighting, dense environmental detail, sparkling reflections, glowing lanterns, cinematic atmosphere, and rich blue-orange color contrast. Include Japanese poster typography integrated into the art: at the very top, the tagline "ひとりで生きてきた。だけど、ひとりじゃ涙は止まらない。"; above the title, the line "独身オヤジ、最後の青春。"; a very large main title at the bottom center reading "翼のオヤジ" in bold brushed calligraphic characters; below it, the tagline "笑って、泣けて、明日また頑張れる。この冬、いちばんやさしい奇跡。"; on the bottom right, a circular badge reading "秋公開" and "今"; add small fine-print credits across the lower edge in the style of a Japanese film poster. ![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Ay'da tuhaf bir sentoyu tasvir eden retro-fütüristik bir anime çizgi roman sayfası; birden fazla karakter odaklı panel içeren eğlenceli AI manga sahneleri oluşturmak için ideal.

#### 📝 İstem

```
A colorful single-page Japanese comic manga set in a whimsical lunar public bathhouse on the moon, drawn in a polished retro-futuristic anime style with warm lighting, thick clean panel borders, expressive sound effects, and highly detailed environmental storytelling. The scene is a moon onsen called "月面銭湯 つきのゆ" with a large illuminated entrance sign, blue noren curtain with the white character "ゆ", exposed pipes, gauges, rounded architecture, and a giant circular window showing the moon surface and Earth in space. Include exactly 8 comic panels arranged in a dynamic page layout. Panel 1: exterior establishing shot of the bathhouse on the moon, with the sign "月面銭湯 つきのゆ", a smaller sign reading "重力 1/6", a red milk vending machine labeled "牛乳", a tanuki statue, lunar terrain outside, and a vertical banner promoting the bath. Panel 2: a young female mechanic bathhouse worker with {argument name="character design" default="brown ponytail tied with a red polka-dot bandana, green work jumpsuit, tool belt, energetic expression"} adjusts a machine or boiler control, seen from behind or side, with speech balloons about preparing today's bath and boiler condition. Panel 3: a cute alien customer with {argument name="alien appearance" default="round mint-green body, purple spots, sleepy eyes, pink cheeks, small mouth, white towel with a purple star on its head"} relaxes in steaming bathwater, half submerged, with a rubber duck floating nearby and a wooden sign reading "ぬるめ じっくり リラックス". Panel 4: a small cleaning robot with {argument name="robot design" default="silver body, blue accents, black digital face with glowing blue eyes, red antenna light, thin mechanical arms and legs"} happily scrubs the floor with broom and bucket beside a hanging sign that says "清掃中". Panel 5: the same robot suddenly slips or splashes dramatically into the bath, with a huge water burst, many bubbles, the large sound effect "ぽわぁ〜ん!!", and the worker reacting in surprise from the side. Panel 6: the worker sits by the bath smiling, holding a bottle labeled "月面牛乳". Panel 7: the alien in the bath gives a thumbs-up while holding a bottle labeled "月面フルーツオーレ", looking blissfully satisfied, with the rubber duck still present. Panel 8: the cheerful robot poses beside the bath with cleaning tools and a bucket, near a bath curtain marked "ゆ" and a pink wash basin labeled "つきのゆ", saying the bath is the best. Maintain a cozy, comedic tone, retro Showa-style sento details mixed with space technology, glossy tiled bath surfaces, steam, bubbles, and cute character acting throughout. The comic should feel like a charming slice-of-life gag manga about working at a lunar bathhouse.
```

The bottle is clear with condensation, a white cap, visible water inside, and a deep blue label reading “POCARI SWEAT” in large white letters with smaller text above saying “ION SUPPLY DRINK.” Add energetic frozen water splashes and droplets around the bottle, hand, and lower foreground to emphasize freshness and hydration. Across the top, add huge distressed white Korean headline text, slightly angled and filling most of the upper half: {argument name="headline text" default="갈증 해소? 이걸로 끝! 포카리스웨트!"}. In the lower right over the suit, add a bold italic quotation in white and blue Korean text: {argument name="quote" default="WINNING은 수분 싸움! 포카리스웨트로 리프레시!"}. In the bottom left, include exactly 3 circular benefit icons stacked vertically with short Korean labels: a water drop icon with “수분 보충”, a lightning bolt icon with “전해질 보충”, and a running figure icon with “빠른 흡수”. Use a high-contrast, patriotic blue-and-white color palette, dramatic ad lighting, sharp focus on the bottle and hand, slightly softer focus on the face and background, and an overall energetic premium campaign-poster look.

### No. 26: Kore Pirinç İçeceği Parodi Reklam Posteri

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Bu prompt, ünlü bir politikacı benzeri sözcünün Kore usulü konserve pirinç içeceğini tanıttığı komik, yüksek etkili bir parodi içecek reklam posteri oluşturur.

#### 📝 İstem

```
Create a bold Korean-style beverage advertisement poster with a warm golden splash background and dramatic commercial lighting. Show a {argument name="celebrity spokesperson" default="Donald Trump-like older male politician"} from the chest up, wearing a navy suit, white dress shirt, bright red tie, and a small American flag lapel pin, facing camera with a confident sales-pitch expression. His face is obscured by a flat rectangular censor block in a skin-toned color. In his left hand, extended close to the camera in forced perspective, he holds a yellow aluminum can of Korean rice punch drink labeled prominently in Korean, with red top and bottom bands and the main product text "비락 식혜" and "Since 1993" on the can. The can also includes smaller Korean copy, an image of sweet rice drink near the bottom, and the volume text "238 ml (120 kcal)". His right hand gives a thumbs-up.

Use an energetic retro-commercial composition, with splashing sweet rice beverage and droplets behind him, glowing golden highlights, and a slightly low-angle heroic framing. At the top, include 3 distinct headline text groups: a small handwritten-style black slogan on the upper left reading "전통의 맛, 한국의 DRINK!", a huge central headline in distressed bold Korean type reading "걸죽는 땐?" in dark brown-black and "비락 식혜!" in vivid red, and a brand logo on the upper right reading "비락" with small red text "Since 1993" beneath it. Add 2 callout badges: on the left, a yellow circular seal with a tiny crown icon and the text "대한민국 국민음료 No.1"; on the right, a white speech bubble with handwritten Korean text "한국이 만든 맛있는 전통!" and red English text "I LOVE IT!".

At the bottom foreground, place 2 food elements: a brass bowl filled with sweet rice drink and floating rice grains on the left, and a wooden bowl piled with white rice on the right. Across the lower middle, add 2 lines of large brush-style promotional text, the first in white reading "달콤하게! 시원하게!" and the second in mixed white and yellow reading "속까지 시~원하게!" with an energetic yellow underline stroke. Along the very bottom, include 3 circular feature icons with captions in Korean: "국내산 쌀 엄선된 재료", "시원하게 갈증해소", and "부드러운 단맛 속 편한 식혜". In the lower right corner, add tiny disclaimer text "연출된 이미지입니다". Make the overall look glossy, exaggerated, funny, and convincing like a viral parody print ad.
```

### No. 29: Japonca Orman Temalı Park Parodi Posteri

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Parodi kampanyaları, sosyal medya görselleri veya sahte tanıtım ana sanat çalışmaları için ideal, kurgusal bir orman dinozor tema parkı için sinematik, hicivli Japonca reklam posteri.

#### 📝 İstem

```
A hyper-detailed Japanese parody theme park advertisement poster in a vertical format, designed like a dramatic summer travel ad mixed with a luxury attraction campaign. The setting is a tropical jungle under a vivid blue sky with scattered clouds and a bright blazing sun in the upper right corner, with palm leaves framing the top edges. Across the top, place a huge 3D stone-textured Japanese headline reading {argument name="headline text" default="ジャンキリア沖縄"}, with a smaller white Japanese tagline underneath that reads "— やんばるの大自然に包まれた、超本格ジャングル・テーマパーク —". In the center, feature a large modern smartphone standing upright and slightly tilted, dominating the composition. On its screen, show a beige ticket-lottery waiting interface with jungle silhouettes at the top and large bold Japanese text reading "整理券抽選中", a circular loading indicator, and smaller text near the bottom reading "結果発表まで30分" and "※この画面を閉じずにお待ちください". The phone status bar should show 10:00. Behind the phone on the left, place a roaring Tyrannosaurus rex emerging from jungle foliage, mouth open wide, realistic and threatening. On the right, place an ornate golden entrance gate with detailed carvings and a sign reading "プレミアムパス入口", leading to a red-carpeted premium entry lane. In the foreground and midground, show a long crowded queue of park visitors stretching deep into the scene, all wearing casual summer clothing, hats, towels, backpacks, and carrying umbrellas, fans, and water bottles, suggesting extreme heat and exhaustion. Several people nearest the viewer should have blurred faces. On the far left, add a giant weathered stone sign with huge red Japanese text reading "待ち時間 180分". At the lower left, include 3 stacked rustic wooden signboards: the top sign has a blue parking icon and text "駐車場 2,000円"; the middle sign has a smartphone icon and text "アプリ必須 ダウンロードしてね!"; the bottom sign has a dinosaur silhouette and text "当選者だけが冒険へ". Along the lower right side, place very large vertical white brush-style Japanese copy reading "待つこと、それが冒険だ。". Near the bottom right, include 3 small circular icon callouts with short Japanese promotional lines: "抽選に選ばれし者だけが、恐竜に会える。", "スマホの充電が尽きる前に、夢は始まる。", and "プレミアムな近道も、ご用意しました。" with icons suggesting dinosaur, phone battery, and VIP access. At the very bottom center, add a black disclaimer strip with small white Japanese text reading "このポスターは架空のパロディ広告です". The overall style should be ultra-realistic, cinematic, high-contrast, satirical, and polished like a premium commercial poster, with exaggerated theme park hype, oppressive heat, and absurd queue-based adventure as the core joke.
```

### No. 31: Canlı Dünya'nın Yanındaki Astronot

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Bu prompt, köklerle kaplı bir Dünya'nın yanında yalnız bir astronotun süzüldüğü, kasvetli ve sinematik bir bilimkurgu görseli oluşturur; sürreal uzay sanatı veya AI temalı editoryal görseller için idealdir.

```

### No. 33: Steampunk Vintage Video Platformu Kullanıcı Arayüzü

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Açıklama

#### 📝 İstem

```
Create a full-screen fictional video platform homepage in a richly detailed steampunk Victorian style, designed like an antique brass-and-wood web interface with dark bronze metal frames, engraved ornament, rivets, pipes, exposed gears, glowing Edison bulbs, and sepia-toned textures throughout. At the top center, a large embossed title reads {argument name="site name" default="ElectroVid"} in ornate gold serif lettering on a dark plaque, with a smaller subtitle plaque beneath it reading "THE FUTURE IN MOTION". In the top left corner, overlay a modern brand mark reading "Pollo AI" and "GPT Image 2" in clean contemporary type, contrasting with the antique interface. Add a circular analog gauge in the top right corner. Below the header, place a navigation bar with exactly 6 items: a home icon, "TRENDING", "INNOVATIONS", "DOCUMENTARIES", "ENTERTAINMENT", and a search field showing {argument name="search placeholder" default="Search ElectroVid..."} plus a search icon. The main layout is two-column: a narrow left sidebar and a larger main content area. In the left sidebar, add a section titled "POPULAR CHANNELS" containing exactly 3 vertically stacked channel cards, each with a circular emblem, channel name, subscriber count, and a "SUBSCRIBE" button: "THE PATENT OFFICE" with "27.4K SUBSCRIBERS", "THE ROYAL SOCIETY" with "18.7K SUBSCRIBERS", and "GENERAL ELECTRIC" with "35.1K SUBSCRIBERS". In the main content area, feature a large central video player framed in ornate brass. The paused video image is a sepia historical scene of two suited men debating in front of a chalkboard marked "AC vs. DC" with lightning sketches, one man pointing and the other gesturing, with soft blurred censor blocks over both faces. Include a video progress bar and controls along the bottom edge of the player, and a timestamp reading "08:47 / 22:31". Beneath the player, show the title {argument name="featured video title" default="The Truth About AC vs. DC: The Final Debate"} in large serif text, followed by channel metadata for "The Electrical Age", "142K views", and "3 days ago", plus a like button on the right labeled "LIKE" and "5.8K". Below that, create a section header reading "LATEST VIDEOS" and display exactly 3 thumbnail cards in one row. Card 1 shows a sepia portrait of Thomas Edison holding a glowing bulb with duration "10:12", title "My New Incandescent Bulb", and metadata "Thomas Edison", "89K views", "5 days ago". Card 2 shows a dramatic sepia image of a Tesla coil tower under electrical arcs with duration "15:36", title "The Wonders of the Wardenclyffe Tower", and metadata "Nikola Tesla", "120K views", "1 week ago". Card 3 shows an antique automobile on a street with duration "12:08", title "The Automobile Revolution", and metadata "Henry Ford", "110K views", "1 week ago". Centered below the row, add a button reading "VIEW ALL VIDEOS". At the bottom center, add a copyright plaque reading "© 1893 ElectroVid, Ltd. All rights reserved.". Use a symmetrical, meticulously crafted interface with realistic depth, embossed typography, subtle warm lighting, old parchment panels, Victorian engraving aesthetics, and a polished cinematic sepia palette of brass, copper, dark wood, blackened steel, and antique gold.

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)

#### 📝 İstem

```
Using the attached character, generate the following:

# Instructions
Create a minimalist theater-style vertical poster for {argument name="user input" default="[user input]"} using monochrome + {argument name="accent color" default="one accent color"}.

# Layout Requirements
- Place the title largely in the bottom 1/4 area, with the Japanese title at maximum size and the English subtitle small directly underneath.
- Place a catchphrase (1-2 lines) in the top center.
- Stack 3-4 awards/official certification badges vertically in the top-left corner.
- Place a vertical catchphrase (2-3 lines) along the right edge.
- Position the main character as a silhouette from behind, slightly left of the center.
- Represent fantastical elements (floating islands, giant creatures) in the background as silhouettes.
- Place staff credits, release date, and distribution info in a small horizontal line at the bottom.
- Highlight the release date in a large font at the bottom right.

# Design Requirements
- Keep the background monochrome (black to gray gradient).
- Use only one accent color (e.g., vivid cobalt blue or gold).
- Combine silhouette and thin line art styles.
- Emphasize the title text with white + the accent color.
- Create a cinematic and artistic atmosphere overall.
- Avoid colorful backgrounds, excessive decoration, or heavy use of gradients.
- Format: Vertical, aspect ratio 2:3, high resolution.
```

### No. 51: Dört Panelli Romantik Komedi Manga Sayfası

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Bu prompt, Japonca diyaloglu, ifade edici karakter oyunculuğuyla dramatik romantik komedi tartışma sahneleri oluşturmak için ideal, tek renkli dört panelli bir manga sayfası oluşturur.

#### 📝 İstem

```
Create a black-and-white manga page with 4 stacked horizontal panels, clean black gutters, screentone shading, dramatic speed lines, and polished seinen-style linework. The page features two youthful anime characters with modern casual clothing and short dark hair, with the face area of both characters obscured by a soft square blur censor block. Panel 1: a slim young person with messy short dark hair and a collared shirt clenches one fist near their chest, body angled left, surrounded by an intense fiery aura effect in the background, looking emotional and defensive. On the right side, place a large jagged vertical speech balloon containing this Japanese text: 「何十時間も魂を削って描いた一枚と、プロンプト打ち込んで数秒で出した画像が同じ価値なわけないでしょ！ふざけないで！」. Panel 2: a second young person with slightly taller build, short dark hair, a dark zip jacket over a light shirt, raises one index finger calmly as if explaining a point. Add a rounded rectangular speech box on the right with this Japanese text: 「投下した労働時間で価値が決まるという典型的な“労働価値説の誤謬”だ。市場における価値は、出力された結果を受け手がどう評価するかで決まる」. Panel 3: the taller character gently pats the shorter character on the head; include a small hand-pat sound effect near the hand reading 「ポン」. The shorter character looks up in surprise. On the right side, add a large oval vertical speech balloon with this Japanese text: 「でも俺の市場価値基準はすごくシンプルだよ。君が俺のために照れてくれるこの数秒間に、何十時間分の価値も感じてるから」. Panel 4: close-up of the shorter character blushing intensely with spiral eyes, sweat drops, trembling expression, open mouth, and dense hatching on the cheeks, overwhelmed with embarrassment. Fill the background with dramatic radiating speed lines. Add a large jagged vertical speech balloon on the right with this Japanese text: 「だ、誰がアンタのために照れるか…っ！自意識過剰よ！」. Add two sound effects: a small 「プル…」 near the shoulder and a larger shaky handwritten 「カァァァ」 along the lower left side. Keep the whole page monochrome, highly expressive, romantic-comedy manga tone, with strong emotional contrast between heated argument, cool explanation, teasing affection, and flustered payoff.
```

Lighting is soft natural daylight, slightly overcast, with muted colors, shallow depth of field, and a vintage editorial photography look. Composition should be vertical, full seated figure, straight-on, balanced, and quietly uncanny. ### No. 59: Referans Salonuna Anime Kızı Ekle

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Bu istem, orijinal oda kompozisyonunu koruyarak, sağlanan gerçek bir iç mekan arka planına büyük bir anime kız karakteri yerleştirir; karakter birleştirme testleri veya arka plan referans deneyleri için uygundur.

#### 📝 İstem

```
Using the provided reference image as the exact background base, keep the same upscale modern lounge/game-room interior, preserving the room layout, perspective, lighting mood, foosball table, chess table, shelves, pendant lamps, and seating. Add a large anime-style girl in the foreground, centered slightly right and filling most of the frame from thighs up, composited naturally into the scene with correct perspective and soft ambient lighting that matches the room. She should have {argument name="hair color" default="silver-lavender"} long twin-tails tied with black ribbons, wear a black-and-white gothic lolita dress with a frilled white blouse, black bow at the collar, black corset waist, and ribbon accents on the sleeves, and make a peace sign with one hand near her face. Render her in polished modern anime illustration style, with detailed hair strands and fabric folds, while leaving the background photorealistic. Cover the face with a plain square mosaic/censor block in the center of the head area. Keep the camera angle close to the original room view and make the added character feel naturally placed in front of the chess table and armchair.
```

### No. 63: Retro Piksel Dağ Vadisi

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Yarım ton çizgi roman gölgelendirmeli, canlı bir piksel sanatı alp manzarası; retro oyun arka planları, manzara posterleri veya nostaljik çevre sanatı için idealdir.

#### 📝 İstem

```
A highly detailed retro pixel art landscape of a bright alpine valley in summer, composed like a classic side-scrolling video game background but shown as a wide scenic vista. In the foreground, a winding tan dirt path curves from the bottom center into the middle distance through dense wildflower meadows, with a small blue stream at the lower right bordered by gray rocks and lush grass. Count 2 large foreground rock clusters, 1 winding path, and 1 visible stream. Fill the meadows with colorful flowers in vivid purple, yellow, red, pink, and white, with especially tall purple flower spikes on the left foreground and dense mixed blossoms on both sides of the path. On the left and right midground, place thick stands of leafy green trees and dark pine trees, framing the open valley center. In the background, show a dramatic mountain range with exactly 7 visible peaks: 1 dominant tall snow-capped peak slightly right of center, 2 medium purple peaks to its left, 2 smaller snowy blue peaks in the far center distance, 1 smaller purple peak to the right, and 1 cropped rocky mountain edge at the far left. Use vibrant greens and purples as the main palette, with cool blue shadows and lavender mountain faces. Above, render a bright blue sky with large creamy white clouds, halftone-dot shading throughout the sky and mountains, subtle vintage comic print texture, visible dithering, and crisp sharp pixel edges. Add exactly 4 small flying bird silhouettes in the sky. The whole image should feel colorful, nostalgic, scenic, and richly layered, with heavy halftone comic shading, retro print grain, no text, no UI, no characters, and no buildings.
```

### No. 67: Japonca Yapay Zeka Modeli Reçete Formu

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Resmi görünümlü parodi belgeleri ve sahte evrak işleri oluşturmak için kullanışlı, bir yapay zeka modeli için mizahi Japonca reçete formunun gerçekçi bir üstten çekim fotoğrafı.

#### 📝 İstem

```
{
  "type": "Japanese prescription document parody",
  "style": "photorealistic overhead document photo",
  "subject": "a single white prescription sheet printed in Japanese, placed on a warm-toned wooden tabletop",
  "document": {
    "paper": {
      "size": "A4 portrait",
      "color": "white",
      "orientation": "slightly rotated clockwise",
      "condition": "clean flat sheet with subtle natural paper texture"
    },
    "print": {
      "ink": "black with one red seal box",
      "font": "Japanese Mincho-style serif mixed with simple sans-serif table text",
      "linework": "thin gray-black ruled boxes and dividers"
    },
    "header": {
      "title": "処方箋",
      "subtitle": "（この処方箋は、大規模言語モデル用です）",
      "date_label": "発行日：",
      "date_value": "{argument name=\"issue date\" default=\"2025年6月5日\"}"
    },
    "top_fields": {
      "count": 6,
      "items": [
        { "label": "患者名", "value": "{argument name=\"patient name\" default=\"ChatGPT\"}" },
        { "label": "性別", "value": "N/A" },
        { "label": "年齢", "value": "N/A" },
        { "label": "モデル名", "value": "{argument name=\"model name\" default=\"GPT-5.4 Thinking\"}" }
      ]
    },
    "main_section": {
      "left_title": "持病・症状（大規模言語モデル特有の持病）",
      "left_count": 8,
      "left_items": [
        "1．幻覚（Hallucination）傾向",
        "2．知識のカットオフによる情報の陳腐化",
        "3．バイアス（学習データ由来の偏見）",
        "4．プロンプトに対する過剰適応（迎合傾向）",
        "5．長文での一貫性の低下",
        "6．複雑な推論時の論理飛躍",
        "7．不確実性の過小評価（自信過剰）",

#### 📖 Açıklama

```
A realistic overhead product photograph on a warm wooden tabletop showing 6 medical-style items neatly arranged in two rows, designed as a humorous Japanese pharmacy set for ChatGPT. Top row: 3 white prescription envelopes standing vertically, each with blue printed borders and Japanese medical typography. Bottom row: 2 blister packs of tablets and 1 small transparent zip bag of white powder, each aligned beneath the corresponding envelope. The paper and packaging should look authentic, like real Japanese clinic dispensing materials, with slight wrinkles, soft natural indoor lighting, and subtle shadows.

Dosage lines indicate twice daily after morning and evening meals, 1 tablet each time, for 7 days. ### No. 74: VINCO Editoryal Moodboard Ekran Görüntüsü

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Kurgusal bir streetwear ve doğal şarap markası için altı görüntülük bir editoryal moda konseptini gösteren, ekran görüntüsü tarzında bir AI moodboard'u; sanat yönetimi dosyalarını veya kampanya referans panolarını yeniden oluşturmak için kullanışlıdır.

#### 📝 İstem

```
Create a 4:5 editorial fashion lookbook moodboard for a fictional brand called {argument name="brand name" default="VINCO"}. The image is a dark-interface screenshot-style composition with a large rounded charcoal text panel across the upper half and a 2-by-3 grid of six fashion/editorial images in the lower left quadrant. The overall aesthetic blends Italian archival graphic design with late-1990s Southern California streetwear, mixing natural wine culture, skate utility, and sun-faded documentary fashion photography. Use gritty but precise art direction, midday outdoor light, slightly chaotic but disciplined typography, and real-person casting rather than polished fashion-model energy. In the top text panel, show a long white sans-serif creative-direction paragraph describing the shoot, with multiple lines of copy, like an AI prompt or design brief displayed inside a rounded dark gray bubble on a near-black background. In the image grid, include exactly 6 tiles: tile 1 shows a young man in an oversized faded olive T-shirt and dark pants standing in front of an off-white poster-like backdrop with bold {argument name="logo text" default="VINCO"} branding, barcode graphics, and small editorial text; tile 2 is a close-up still life of a dark wine bottle with a minimalist white label reading {argument name="bottle label" default="VINCO"}, photographed in warm sunlight with tactile paper texture and shadow; tile 3 shows a person from the back in a washed olive long-sleeve shirt with large subtle chest or back branding, white shorts, and a yellow hanging tag or sticker element near the top right, posed against a pale wall with blue stripe detail and editorial layout text; tile 4 shows a skateboarder crouching or riding away, photographed from behind, wearing a white T-shirt with a large black graphic block on the back and dark shorts, in golden sun on pavement; tile 5 is a printed wine ephemera flat lay with cream paper and a pale chartreuse-green wine label or booklet reading {argument name="product text" default="Vino Naturale"}, featuring grape illustration, small black text, and layered paper pieces; tile 6 shows a person facing camera in a white T-shirt with a race-bib style chest print reading 97, wearing a fluorescent yellow-green cap with small brand text, standing outdoors with palm trees and bright sky behind them. Keep the six images slightly imperfect and collage-like, as if pulled from a campaign deck or saved references. Use earthy tones throughout: olive, cream, charcoal, sun-bleached white, asphalt gray, muted brown, and one fluorescent yellow-green accent repeated in small details. Include visible interface framing around the composition: a dark app-like background, the lower image grid aligned left, and a rounded gray “Edit” button near the bottom left, plus a small circular icon near the bottom right, reinforcing that this is a screenshot of a generated moodboard rather than a clean standalone poster.
```

### No. 87: Anime Gün Batımı Film Posteri

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Bu prompt, gün batımında bir sahil kasabasına bakan iki öğrenciyi içeren, sinematik ana görseller ve romantik drama tanıtım sanatı için ideal, cilalı bir Japon anime film posteri oluşturur.

#### 📝 İstem

```
A breathtaking anime movie poster at golden-hour sunset, vertical theatrical one-sheet composition, painted in the polished cinematic style of a Makoto Shinkai-inspired youth drama. The scene overlooks a Japanese coastal hillside town descending toward a glowing bay, with the sun low on the horizon and its reflection stretching across calm water. The sky dominates most of the image: a vast deep-blue to lavender twilight gradient filled with countless stars, wispy pink and peach clouds, and one especially bright star near the upper right. In the foreground on the right, a teenage schoolgirl stands in three-quarter side profile facing left toward the sea, shown from mid-thigh up, with shoulder-length dark hair blowing in the breeze, a short-sleeved white sailor-style school blouse, a red ribbon at the collar, and a navy pleated skirt; her expression is contemplative and wistful. Farther down the steep stone stair street in the center-left, a teenage schoolboy stands with his back to the viewer, wearing a short-sleeved white shirt and dark trousers, also looking toward the sunset and ocean. At the lower right, include 1 black cat sitting on a wall or rooftop edge in silhouette, looking toward the town. At the lower left, include 1 old-fashioned streetlamp and a dense cluster of blooming hydrangeas in blue and violet along a stone wall. The town below is packed with tiled rooftops, narrow streets, warm window lights, and layered houses, with distant mountains framing the bay. Use dramatic rim light, luminous atmospheric perspective, sparkling highlights, delicate cloud detail, and emotional, nostalgic color grading in indigo, ultramarine, pink, peach, and gold. Design it explicitly as a Japanese animated film poster with elegant typography integrated into the artwork: large hand-brushed Japanese title text across the upper-left to center reading {argument name="title text" default="星をつなぐ約束のうた"}, smaller English subtitle beneath it reading {argument name="English subtitle" default="The Song of Promises"}, a small award-laurel line in Japanese at the top left, 1 vertical Japanese tagline along the upper-right edge, 4 cast names in Japanese centered near the bottom, a release date at the lower left reading {argument name="release date" default="8.23"} with "ROADSHOW" below, 1 pink Japanese tagline across the lower center, and a website/social handle at the lower right. Ultra-detailed anime key visual, romantic and melancholic, premium feature-film poster finish.
```

### No. 91: Minimal Pelikan Bisiklet Sürüyor

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Bu prompt, basit şekil kompozisyonunu test etmek veya oyuncul, soyut ikon tarzı bir görsel oluşturmak için kullanışlı, bir bisiklet üzerindeki pelikanın sade, geometrik vektör illüstrasyonunu oluşturur.

#### 📝 İstem

```
A minimalist vector-style illustration on a flat light gray background showing a pelican riding a bicycle, drawn from simple geometric shapes with thick dark charcoal outlines. The composition is wide and centered, with the bicycle occupying the lower two-thirds of the image and the bird’s head floating slightly above and forward of the handlebars in a deliberately abstract, diagram-like way. The bicycle is a simple black road-bike silhouette in side view with exactly 2 large wheels, each with a thick outer rim and exactly 4 visible spoke lines forming a cross, a straight horizontal ground line beneath both wheels, a triangular frame, a short black saddle, and simplified crank and pedal details near the rear of the frame. The pelican is constructed from clean abstract pieces: a white rounded head with a small black circular eye, a long open beak pointing left made of 2 parts with an upper orange triangular section and a lower pale pink pouch section, a short dark curve on top of the head, a small separate white oval neck/body connector, a larger white rounded body positioned over the bike, and a single white wing-like shape angled upward over the back. Add exactly 2 orange leg shapes, long narrow rectangles leaning downward from the body toward the bicycle frame, suggesting the bird is pedaling. Keep the forms intentionally sparse and slightly surreal, like a logo test or simple code-editor doodle, with no shading, no gradients, no textures, no text, and lots of negative space.
```

### No. 92: Sevimli Dört Panelli Kedi Kıskançlığı Çizgi Romanı

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Sosyal medya paylaşımları, manga tarzı mizah veya samimi evcil hayvan illüstrasyonları için ideal, sıcak, el yapımı bir dört panelli kedi çizgi romanı oluşturan prompt.

#### 📝 İstem

```
A cute hand-drawn four-panel comic in a soft, warm, slice-of-life style on a light cream background with thick black panel borders and slightly textured paper grain. Use simple rounded cartoon cat anatomy, expressive faces, clean black outlines, muted natural colors, and a gentle manga-like presentation. In the top-left panel, show 2 cats: a brown tabby cat with dark stripes and white muzzle sitting with eyes closed, looking pleased, while a mostly white cat with dark brown patches on the head stands beside it and affectionately licks the tabby's cheek; add 2 small black musical notes above them to suggest happy grooming. In the top-right panel, show the white-and-brown patched cat in the foreground looking toward a small calico kitten standing to the right; include a speech bubble containing the Japanese text "めい" above the kitten. In the bottom-left panel, show 3 cats together: the brown tabby on the left with a surprised or blank expression, the white patched cat on the right looking cheerful, and the small calico kitten centered in front between them, looking up. In the bottom-right panel, show a close-up of the brown tabby cat alone, facing forward with narrowed yellow-green eyes and an angry, jealous expression; add 2 short emphasis lines near the face and 1 small puff-shaped anger symbol to the right. Keep the tone cozy and comedic, with the visual joke that the tabby was happy being groomed until the new kitten appears. Use flat colors, minimal shading, and a charming Japanese webcomic feel.
```

### No. 93: 108 Chibi Fantezi Mandala

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Tam olarak 108 benzersiz chibi mitolojik yaratığın konsantrik mandala halkaları halinde düzenlendiği son derece detaylı geniş fantezi poster; dekoratif anahtar sanat veya sergi illüstrasyonları için ideal.

#### 📝 İstem

```
A gigantic ultra-detailed fantasy mandala poster featuring exactly 108 distinct chibi characters arranged in concentric circular rings around a radiant central emblem. The composition is perfectly symmetrical overall and fills a wide horizontal canvas like an ornate collectible mural. In the center, place a glowing golden core with 9 chibi animal-fantasy mascots clustered in a circular medallion, each with oversized heads, tiny bodies, expressive eyes, and luxurious costume details. Surround this center with multiple evenly spaced concentric rings containing the remaining 99 characters, each character occupying its own wedge-like segment and designed as a unique elemental or mythical variation. Include fox-like, rabbit-like, cat-like, wolf-like, lion-like, bird-like, dragon-like, deer-like, and hybrid beast characters, all rendered in a cute super-deformed style but with epic high-fantasy armor, robes, crowns, feathers, horns, gems, capes, staffs, and magical accessories. Make every character visually distinct through color, silhouette, species traits, and elemental theme, while preserving a unified painterly anime-fantasy aesthetic.

Use a rich palette dominated by luminous gold, ivory, cream, violet, indigo, sapphire, and soft amber, with accents of crimson, icy cyan, emerald, and sunset orange. Give the image the feel of a sacred celestial chart or zodiac wheel, with each circular band separated by elegant gilded borders and arc dividers. Add glowing magical energy, sparkles, halos, swirling fire, mist, snow, clouds, water splashes, lightning curls, floral motifs, and celestial particles around many of the characters. Around the outer perimeter, place several larger decorative guardian illustrations integrated into the border: a bright sun medallion at the upper left, a white phoenix-like bird in a circular panel at the upper right, a floral or starburst medallion at the lower right, and a fiery character cluster in a circular panel at the lower left, plus additional large elemental beast figures embedded along the left and right edges. Frame the entire artwork with an elaborate antique ornamental border inspired by illuminated manuscripts and fantasy tarot designs, using filigree, corner medallions, geometric trim, and arcane motifs.

The rendering should be extremely dense and crisp, like a 4k fantasy illustration meant for a poster print, with tiny readable character silhouettes across the whole image, intricate linework, soft watercolor-textured shading, glowing highlights, and a polished collectible-card-game concept art finish. Emphasize abundance, harmony, and radial order: exactly 108 chibi figures total, arranged as a majestic mandala of mythical elemental mascots.
```

```
A realistic documentary-style photo of an elementary school classroom during a math activity, with about 10 children seated around grouped wooden desks, wearing green and blue school uniforms, actively playing a colorful multiplication domino game. The camera is at child eye level, slightly angled downward toward the main table in the foreground. Center the scene on one square educational board game labeled in Portuguese, with the title "DOMINÓ DA MULTIPLICAÇÃO" on the lower edge and "TREINANDO AS TABUADAS" in the center, surrounded by a border of brightly colored domino-style multiplication tiles. Show 4 children clearly engaged around this main board: one child placing a yellow tile onto the board, one child holding a stack of multicolored tiles, one child watching from the left, and one child in a blue sleeve at the bottom edge arranging pieces. Include 2 shallow wooden boxes labeled "JOGO DE DOMINÓ," one near the center-left and one at the bottom-right, each containing colorful rectangular domino pieces. Scatter school materials naturally on the desks: 3 pencils, 2 worksheets, 1 water bottle, pencil cases, notebooks, and extra game tiles. In the background, show the rest of the classroom softly out of focus with additional students at desks, a bookshelf, a corkboard filled with children’s drawings, and a large multiplication chart poster on the left wall reading "TABUADA DE MULTIPLICAÇÃO." Bright natural daylight enters from tall windows on the right, giving the room a warm, lively, authentic school atmosphere. The educational board and tiles should use vivid classroom colors like yellow, blue, pink, green, and orange. Faces should be unobtrusive or de-emphasized, with the focus on hands-on learning, collaboration, and the multiplication domino activity. Vertical composition, highly realistic photography, candid classroom moment, sharp foreground details, soft depth of field in the background.

### No. 101: Kuşlar ve Hayvanlarla Sürreal Okçu

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Bu prompt, kuşlar ve hayvanlarla çevrili, maskeli bir okçunun rüya gibi sinematik moda tarzı portresini oluşturur; sürreal editöryel veya güzel sanat görseli oluşturma için kullanışlıdır.

#### 📝 İstem

```

### No. 105: Tarihi Buluş Zaman Çizelgesi Izgarası

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Bu prompt, tarih boyunca etiketli buluş dioramalarını gösteren, parşömen tarzında eğitici bir poster oluşturur; zaman çizelgesi infografikleri ve dünyayı değiştiren teknoloji karşılaştırmaları için idealdir.

#### 📝 İstem

```
Create a square infographic-style illustration showing a {argument name="grid size" default="15×15"} invention timeline grid rendered as a collection of miniature isometric dioramas on aged parchment tiles. The image should look like a curated historical poster that spans from {argument name="starting year" default="1000 BC"} to {argument name="ending year" default="2026"}, with one invention per tile and no repeats. Show the visible portion as a 5 by 5 section of the larger grid, for a total of 25 labeled tiles, arranged in neat rows and columns with thin dark borders. Every tile contains a unique world-changing invention depicted as a small handcrafted diorama with era-appropriate materials, colors, and background details. Use a warm antiquarian palette for ancient and medieval inventions, sepia technical-document tones for early modern inventions, and cooler neon-blue futuristic lighting for modern digital and biotech inventions. Surround the grid with an old-map border and subtle historical cartography textures, blending into faint modern network graphics near the bottom right.

Label each visible tile with a small beige caption tag in bold black text. Include exactly these 25 visible inventions in reading order from top left to bottom right: 1) {argument name="first tile label" default="1000 BC"} tile showing an iron plow and simple hand tools in a farm field, captioned "Iron Plow & Tools"; 2) "Concept of Zero" shown as a parchment-like tile with a carved zero symbol and a blue hourglass; 3) "Water Clock" shown as a wooden water-timing device; 4) "Catapult" shown as a wooden siege engine; 5) "Antikythera Mechanism" shown as an intricate bronze gear device in a stone niche; 6) "Concrete" shown as a wheelbarrow filled with wet cement or mortar; 7) "Wheelbarrow" shown as a simple wooden one-wheel cart; 8) "Windmill" shown as a traditional mill on grassy ground; 9) "Gunpowder" shown as a barrel and a mound of black powder with smoke; 10) "Printing Press" shown as a wooden press framed by classical columns; 11) "Mechanical Clock" shown as an ornate standing clock; 12) "Telescope" shown as an early brass telescope on a tripod with sketch-like scientific notes; 13) "Steam Engine" shown on a blue blueprint-style tile with an early locomotive engine; 14) "Electric Battery" shown on a blueprint-like tile with two cylindrical battery cells and wiring; 15) "Telegraph" shown as a Morse telegraph key on technical paper; 16) "Light Bulb" shown glowing warmly on a neutral pedestal; 17) "Automobile" shown as an early red motorcar on a workshop-plan background; 18) "Airplane" shown as a commercial jet aircraft in miniature; 19) "Transistor" shown as a black microchip on a luminous circuit-board tile; 20) "Personal Computer" shown as a beige desktop computer with CRT monitor and keyboard; 21) "World Wide Web" shown as a glowing blue globe over digital circuitry; 22) "Smartphone" shown as a sleek modern phone on a neon-tech background; 23) "CRISPR-Cas9" shown as a DNA double helix in a biotech-blue display tile; 24) "Reusable Rocket" shown as several upright rockets launching with exhaust clouds; 25) "AI (LLMs)" shown as glowing large letters AI in a holographic tech cube; 26) "Brain-Computer Interface" shown as a glowing brain hologram on a blue platform; 27) "Advanced Neural Interface (Implant)" shown as a transparent human head profile with a glowing brain implant, with a small top label reading "2026".

Keep the composition highly organized, poster-like, and visually dense, with each tile readable at a glance. Use slight isometric perspective, crisp linework, painterly shading, and polished editorial illustration quality. The overall feeling should combine museum poster, educational timeline, and imaginative historical-tech diorama art.
```

### No. 110: Çanakkale'nin Minik Gezegen Havadan Görünümü

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Bu prompt, Çanakkale'nin sahil şeridi simgelerinin gerçekçi bir 360 derecelik minik-gezegen drone görüntüsünü oluşturur; seyahat görselleri ve şehir poster görselleri için idealdir.

#### 📝 İstem

```
A dramatic ultra-wide aerial tiny-planet photograph of {argument name="city name" default="Canakkale"}, Turkey, rendered as a full 360-degree stereographic projection so the city and waterfront form a compact spherical world surrounded by a swirling ring of blue sky and white clouds. The viewpoint is high above the shoreline in bright daytime with crisp summer light, realistic colors, and strong photographic detail. Place the large hillside sign reading {argument name="landmark sign text" default="Canakkale"} prominently across the center of the miniature planet. On the left-upper side of the sphere, show a tall pale stone clock tower with a small red Turkish flag at the top, surrounded by dense urban blocks with red-tiled roofs and mid-rise buildings. On the right side, include a vivid blue harbor with 2 white passenger ferries docked along the waterfront and a long curving coastline extending into the distance. In the lower-right quadrant, feature the monumental dark wooden Trojan horse statue on a circular plaza. In the lower-left quadrant, include the large rectangular concrete memorial structure set within green parkland. Cover the planet with winding pedestrian paths, lawns, trees, and landscaped gardens, with city streets and waterfront promenades visible around the edges. Use a highly realistic drone-photo look, deep depth of field, sharp textures, slightly exaggerated fisheye distortion from the tiny-planet projection, and a majestic travel-poster composition emphasizing the contrast between the green park, historic landmarks, and sparkling sea.
```

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Bu prompt, kasvetli, kayalık bir kanyonda, sinematik konsept sanatı ve yaratık tasarımı için ideal, gerçekçi bir insansı uzaylının rahatsız edici tam vücut bilimkurgu korku portresini oluşturur.

```

The creature is extremely tall and emaciated, with elongated limbs, narrow shoulders, a sunken torso, visible rib-like structures, taut sinewy anatomy, long forearms, oversized hands with long thin fingers, and long digitigrade-looking feet planted on wet black ground. Its skin is hairless, slick, pale gray-beige with brownish fleshy undertones, semi-organic and biomechanical in appearance, with glossy damp highlights, leathery textures, stretched membranes, tendons, grooves, and subtle vein-like striations. The neck and upper chest are fused into a disturbing organic structure, with tendril-like folds and open channels running from the clavicle area upward into the head. The head is broad and mushroom- or hammer-shaped with a ridged crown and flared side lobes, giving a nonhuman silhouette; the face should feel unreadable and alien rather than cute or familiar. Place the figure in a narrow canyon of dark eroded stone, with 2 large foreground rock masses framing the subject on the left and right, and a misty cliff wall receding behind it. Use cold desaturated lighting, soft fog, damp surfaces, shallow atmospheric haze, and a grim monochrome palette of charcoal, slate, ash gray, and muted flesh tones. The mood should be uncanny, realistic, oppressive, and biologically plausible, like a high-end sci-fi horror still. Ultra-detailed photorealism, sharp texture on the creature, subtle depth of field, dramatic natural backlight from above, no clothing, no tools, no background creatures, no gore, no text.

On the horizon, slightly right of center, a sinister dark castle rises from a lone hill. The sky is filled with enormous turbulent storm clouds, with 3 flying creatures or birds silhouetted in the distance and a break in the clouds casting cold, sickly light across the landscape. Use a grim, painterly, highly detailed style with muted sepia, charcoal, umber, and gray tones, dramatic atmospheric perspective, cinematic composition, and the mood of a foreboding fantasy frontier outpost at the edge of a dead world.

### No. 118: Epik Senna vs Prost Gladyatör Posteri

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Senna ve Prost'u efsanevi gladyatör rakipler olarak betimleyen, dramatik vintage tarzı bir motor sporları posteri; sinematik saygı duruşu sanatını yeniden yaratmak veya yüksek etkili F1 efsanesi posterleri için idealdir.

#### 📝 İstem

```
An epic cinematic poster in a dark golden bronze palette, styled like a mythic gladiator movie poster merged with vintage Formula 1 iconography. Two legendary rival drivers face away from each other in mirrored side-profile bust portraits at the top half of the image, one on the left inspired by Ayrton Senna and one on the right inspired by Alain Prost, both depicted as heroic Roman gladiators with weathered bronze armor, dramatic shoulder plates, and racing colors draped as cloaks. The left figure wears green, yellow, and blue accents, and the right figure wears blue, white, and red accents. Their faces are mostly in shadow, lit by intense backlight through storm clouds, creating a solemn, monumental mood. Behind each driver hangs 1 vertical banner, for a total of 2 banners: the left banner is dark green with a large gold S, the text "SENNA", "#12", and a cursive signature; the right banner is dark blue with a large gold P, the text "PROST", "#1", and a cursive signature. Centered near the top, in elegant serif French text, place the line "DEUX LÉGENDES. UN SEUL TRÔNE." with a small gold Formula 1 emblem and laurel motif below it. In the central sky, add 2 stacked lines of French text reading "RIVAUX SUR LA PISTE." and "LÉGENDES POUR TOUJOURS." The main title dominates the middle in huge metallic serif lettering: "{argument name="headline text" default="SENNA vs PROST"}", with a sword-like vertical separator for "vs". Beneath it, a subtitle in French reads "LE COMBAT ULTIME DE LA F1". The lower half shows a colossal Roman colosseum packed with spectators, flags, arches, dust, smoke, and dramatic perspective lines converging on the center. At the exact center of the arena stands 1 large victory banner with the words "VICTOIRE GLOIRE HONNEUR" in gold. In the foreground, place 2 front-facing late-1980s Formula 1 cars charging toward the viewer on a dirt-covered arena floor, throwing dust. The left car is associated with Senna and features red-and-white Marlboro-inspired livery, Shell branding, and the number 12 on the nose, with the driver wearing a yellow helmet. The right car is associated with Prost and features matching red-and-white Marlboro-inspired livery, Shell branding, and the number 1 on the nose, with the driver wearing a white helmet. At the very bottom, add the line "1988. 1989. 1990." and below it "L’HISTOIRE S’ÉCRIT À PLUS DE 300 KM/H." Include a small ornamental laurel decoration under the final line. Use hyper-detailed textures, dramatic storm clouds, god rays, flying dust, intense contrast, symmetrical composition, ultra-polished poster design, heroic scale, and a timeless legendary atmosphere.
```

### No. 119: Çilekli Dondurma ile Stüdyo Portresi

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Bu prompt, yüzünün önünde çilekli dondurma külahı tutan koyu saçlı bir kadının şık, ünlü tarzı bir stüdyo portresini oluşturur; editoryal güzellik veya pop-kültür görselleri için idealdir.

#### 📝 İstem

```
A polished studio portrait of a glamorous pop-star-like woman from the chest up, centered against a smooth neutral gray backdrop. She has {argument name="hair color" default="jet black"} long loose wavy hair with a middle part, glossy shine, and soft volume falling over both shoulders. Her face is mostly hidden behind the ice cream cone she is holding up in front of her mouth and lower face, creating a playful fashion-editorial composition. She wears a white ribbed tank top with wide straps and a single visible sparkling stud earring. In her hand is 1 waffle cone topped with 1 large scoop of pink strawberry ice cream with dark red berry swirls and slight melting texture. Warm, flattering beauty lighting, soft shadows, realistic skin tones, high-end celebrity portrait photography, crisp focus on the hand, cone, hair, and shoulders, minimal background, subtly sensual and chic mood, vertical crop.
```

### No. 120: Yıldırım Fırlatan Fırtına Büyücüsü

![Language-TR-TR](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-TR-TR-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Açıklama

Fırtına aydınlatması ve çatırdayan büyülü enerji ile dramatik bir büyücü portresi oluşturmak için sinematik, fotogerçekçi bir fantezi prompt'u.

#### 📝 İstem

```
A dramatic dark-fantasy portrait of an elderly wizard standing in a stormy wasteland under a black, cloud-choked sky. He wears a tall, weathered pointed hat with a brown leather band and a tiny metal clasp, and a heavy dark blue-gray robe with wide sleeves. His face is mostly hidden in shadow beneath the hat brim, with long strands of glowing {argument name="accent hair color" default="electric blue"} hair peeking out at the sides and a very long flowing silver-white beard reaching down his chest. The wizard thrusts his left hand toward the camera in a powerful forced-perspective pose, fingers spread, conjuring a bright orb of blue-white magical energy in his palm with crackling lightning arcs wrapping around the hand and sleeve. In his right arm he clutches a large ancient leather spellbook with worn corners, metal fittings, embossed arcane markings on the cover, and a few pages visible. The background shows a barren dark landscape and exactly 1 prominent lightning bolt striking on the right side of the frame. Cinematic high-contrast lighting, hyper-detailed skin and fabric texture, moody photorealism, sharp focus on the hand and beard, intense fantasy atmosphere, centered composition, square crop.
```

## 🤝 Nasıl Katkıda Bulunulur

Katkıları memnuniyetle karşılıyoruz! İstemleri şu yollarla gönderebilirsiniz:

### 🐛 GitHub Issue

1. Click [**Yeni İstem Gönder**](https://github.com/AtlasCloudAI/awesome-gpt-image-2-prompts/issues/new?template=prompt.yml)
2. Formu istem detayları ve görsel ile doldurun
3. Gönderin ve ekip incelemesini bekleyin
4. Onaylanırsa (`approved` etiketi ekleyeceğiz), otomatik olarak CMS'e senkronize edilecektir
5. İsteminiz 4 saat içinde README'de görünecektir

**Not:** Kalite kontrolünü sağlamak için yalnızca GitHub Issues aracılığıyla gönderimleri kabul ediyoruz.

Detaylı yönergeler için [CONTRIBUTING.md](docs/CONTRIBUTING.md) dosyasına bakın.
